AOW_btn_export_data = {
	potential = { always = yes }
	allow = { #别在同一天导出数据了，不好处理
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "AOW_text_do_not_export_data_on_the_same_day"
			NOT = { has_country_flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_is_exporting_data }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_export_data_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			AOW_eft_GLBL_export_data = yes
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = AOW_flag_CNTR_is_exporting_data days = 2 }
		}
	}
}


#默认设置
AOW_btn_preinstall_default_1 = {
	potential = { from = { check_variable = { which = AOW_var_page value = 2 } } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_default_1_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			AOW_eft_GLBL_default_balance_variable = { TYPE = set }
		}
	}
}

#自定义
AOW_btn_preinstall_custom = {
	potential = { from = { check_variable = { which = AOW_var_page value = 2 } } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_custom_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			inline_script = AOW_btn_preinstall_custom/game
		}
	}
}

#零者
AOW_btn_preinstall_laquly = {
	potential = { from = { check_variable = { which = AOW_var_page value = 2 } } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_laquly_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = can_dismantle_megastructure_at_war#允许战争中拆除巨构
			set_global_flag = AOW_flag_GLBL_hyperdimension_hiding#允许研究超维褶皱
			#平衡数值
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 0 }#AI巨构花费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 0 }#AI巨构维护费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }#AI巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 0 }#AI巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }#AI巨构同时建造上限
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = 0 }#玩家巨构花费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = 0 }#玩家巨构维护费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 0 }#玩家巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 0 }#玩家巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 0 }#玩家巨构同时建造上限
				#小型巨构上限（VP是玩家数值，VA是AI数值）
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }#星状开采站
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = space_arena }#星光竞技场
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = space_sensor_station }#星空传感站
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = habitat }#居住站
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = -1 KEY = hyper_relay }#超空间中继器

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = orbital_arc_furnace }#电弧熔炉

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = interstellar_assembly }#星际集会
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 5 KEY = mega_art_installation }#巨构艺术

#6.2
AOW_btn_preinstall_6.2 = {
	potential = { from = { check_variable = { which = AOW_var_page value = 2 } } }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = AOW_btn_preinstall_default_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = can_dismantle_megastructure_at_war#禁止战争中拆除巨构
			set_global_flag = AOW_flag_GLBL_hyperdimension_hiding#禁止研究超维褶皱
			#平衡数值
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_cost value = 3 }#AI巨构花费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_upkp value = 3 }#AI巨构维护费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 20 }#AI巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 1 }#AI巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 30 }#AI巨构同时建造上限
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = 0 }#玩家巨构花费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = 3 }#玩家巨构维护费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 1 }#玩家巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 10 }#玩家巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 100 }#玩家巨构同时建造上限
				#小型巨构上限（VP是玩家数值，VA是AI数值）
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 1 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }#星状开采站

				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_prdc value = 0 }#AI巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_speed value = 0 }#AI巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_ai_mega_build_cap value = 0 }#AI巨构同时建造上限
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_cost value = -0.5 }#玩家巨构花费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_upkp value = -0.5 }#玩家巨构维护费
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_prdc value = 10 }#玩家巨构产出
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_speed value = 30 }#玩家巨构建造速度
				set_variable = { which = AOW_var_player_mega_build_cap value = 60 }#玩家巨构同时建造上限
				#小型巨构上限（VP是玩家数值，VA是AI数值）
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 4 KEY = asteroid_mining_station }#星状开采站
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 3 KEY = space_arena }#星光竞技场

				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = hyper_relay }#超空间中继器
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = orbital_ring }#星环
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = gateway }#星门
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 0 KEY = satellite_defense_base }#卫星防御基地
				AOW_eft_set_mega_cap = { VP = -1 VA = 3 KEY = dyson_swarm }#戴森云

			event_target:global_event_country = {
